  197. Beware that if you are a first time Lactic Acid peel user....this will BURN your face if not done properly. I have done a lot of acid peels from Perfect Image and this one is by far the strongest.<br /><br />I made the mistake of putting it somewhat close to my eyes (like on my dark cirlces\slashes under my eyes). It immediately burned it and became very red. Do not make the same mistake as I did. That skin is way too thin and sensitive to have this strong of a acid peel on it. Before you apply the peel, swipe your face with alcohol on a cotton ball and put vasoline under your eyes, around your nostrils, and your lips. They apply the peel ( i used the little fan brush that they recommend). Leave it on for only a minute for your first time, then rinse your face with room temperature water. If you're face is still burning and feels like needles are prickling your face, mix up a little baking soda and water (to make a paste like consistency) and gently smear all over your face to neutralize the peel. Leave it on for a minute or so, the gently rinse off.<br /><br />I used a vitamin c serum and a very good moisturizer afterwards. Thankfully the combination of those two prevented me from severely ruining the skin under my eyes.<br /><br />It's a little scary, but if done correctly and patiently, the outcome it fantastic. I have fair skin with a LOT of freckles. I've only done the peel twice, and I have noticed a dramatic difference in the coloration of the freckles. Hopefully after a few more peels, they will fade away. Make sure you use a sunscreen if you're going outside. The higher spf the better.
